***родить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a> (2729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rodìti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рождать.html>рожда́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожать.html>рожа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give birth</li>
<li>to give rise to</li>
<li>to bear, to yield <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of land</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The usage of this verb in the imperfective is dated. Modern Russian allows only the use as a perfective.</li></ul>

***родиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:родиться.html>роди́ться</a> (1260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родиться.html>роди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рождаться.html>рожда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be born
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:родиться.html>роди́лся</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:родиться.html>родился́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> 1967 (<a href = vnd.unilang:тысяча.html>ты́сяча</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:девятьсот.html>девятьсо́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шестьдесят.html>шестьдеся́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:седьмой.html>седьмо́м</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>году́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>rodílsja/rodilsjá</b> v 1967 (týsjača devjatʹsót šestʹdesját sedʹmóm) godú.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He was born in 1967.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to arise, to come into being</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родиться.html>роди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li>to sprout, to grow, to germinate, to yield at harvest

Forest Raised a Christmas Tree | ”:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лесу́</a> <b><a ***роднить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:роднить.html>родни́ть</a> (24642)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родня.html>родня́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rodnjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роднить.html>родни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rodnítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сродни́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">породни́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make related
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">породни́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">porodnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bring closer together
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сродни́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">srodnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be in common <i>(between)</i>, to create an affinity <i>(between)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подруга.html>подру́г</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:роднить.html>родни́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:музыка.html>му́зыке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podrúg <b>rodníla</b> ljubóvʹ k múzyke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">their love of music created an affinity between the friends</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li>tribal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:родовой.html>родово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>строй</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rodovój</b> stroj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>tribal</b> system</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>generic

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:родство.html>родство́</a> (10698)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родство.html>родство́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rodstvó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родство.html>родства́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>relationship, kinship, affinity <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">family relationship through marriage of a relative</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>kin</li>
<li>consanguinity, cognation</li>
<li>connection, connexion</li>
<li>alliance</li>
<li>blood</li>
<li>propinquity</li>
<li>cousinage</li></ol>

***рожа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́жа</a> (3493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*roďa</i>, related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rodъ</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">рожаи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rožai</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">appearance, face</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́жа</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">róža</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́жи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́ж</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> face, mug, ugly mug, puss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скорчить.html>ско́рчить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>рожу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skórčitʹ rožu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">make a face</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жо́па</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́жа</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U nevó, što žópa, što <b>róža</b>, odnó i tó že</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You can’t tell his ass from his face.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">licó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">neutral</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A Pan-European formation in medical symptomatology after the appearance of the rose-blossom, compare the translations of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">erysipelas</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́жа</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">róža</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́жи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́ж</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>erysipelas</li></ol>

***рожать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рожать.html>рожа́ть</a> (7320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ражати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ražati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*raďati</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рождать.html>рожда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">roždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожать.html>рожа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rožátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give birth, to bear</li></ol>

***рождать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рождать.html>рожда́ть</a> (8643)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">раждати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raždati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*raďati</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожать.html>рожа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rožátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рождать.html>рожда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">roždátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give birth</li>
<li>to give rise to</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of land</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to bear, to yield</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рождающий.html>рожда́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">roždájuščij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́нье</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énʹje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рожон.html>рожо́н</a> (16975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*oržьnь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожон.html>рожо́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rožón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожон.html>рожна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожон.html>рожны́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожон.html>рожно́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pointed stake <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">placed at an angle in a defensive fortification</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> trouble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рожон.html>рожо́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">leztʹ na <b>rožón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ask for trouble, act recklessly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***рожь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рожь.html>рожь</a> (21328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rъžь</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wrugʰyo-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">raž</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">ръж</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rǎž</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">rudzi</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Roggen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rye</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рожь.html>рожь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rožʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ржать.html>ржи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ржать.html>ржи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ржа.html>ржей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">singular</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rye <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">grass; grain</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stand or field of rye</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роза.html>ро́за</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">róza</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роза.html>ро́зы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роза.html>ро́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роза.html>ро́з</a></b>)
